ART GALLERY THEMES

The Art Gallery is one of many contests that the Neopets site has to offer. For this one, you submit some of your own original Neopets fan art. If your image is selected, it will be placed and honored in the Art Gallery! You'll also get a shiny trophy for your user lookup, 10,000 neo and a random rare item!

Getting Selected

Kikocat selects which works will appear in the competition and it isn't so easy to be selected. When a Neopian holiday is coming up such as Gadgadsbogen, Krawk Day, or Jhudora Day, the Art Gallery is almost always themed around that day, so if one of those are coming up you should submit artwork related to it for a better chance! The same goes for real holidays like Valentines or St. Patrick's.

However, if you do plan to submit your art for a holiday, it's best if you submit it 2 days!! in advance. Often times the Art Gallery sets up its art the day before the actual holiday. Just another reason why it's usually not a good idea to wait till the last minute!

OFFICIAL RULES SUBMIT ENTRY If your picture is published, you will earn 10,000 NP, a rare item, and a trophy for your cabinet.

Contests & Spotlights: http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=spotlights

Food Fight Friday

Quirky Aesthetic is bringing back Food Fight Friday after a full-month of Trick or Treating this past November! Join us once again every Friday for food tosses, chat, friends, giveaways and more! Participate in these events each friday by posting 'food fight friday' in our main guild chat and sending themed food items to other active posting members.

themes

  • Friday, Jan 14th : Sloth Day & Villainous Foods
  • Friday, Jan 21st : Cosmic Cocktail Party
  • Friday, Jan 28th : Kreludor - Moon Grub
  • Friday, Feb 4th : Shenkuu Cuisine

    01 | Scoreboard Reset

    The high score tables reset at around 12:10 AM NST on the 1st of each month; the first day is the easiest to get a trophy, especially in luck/chance games and games with a maximum possible score. Trophies are awarded at 8pm NST each evening. For the best chance at a trophy, send game scores between 12:01am - 7:59pm on the first of the month.

    A few games, namely Maths Nightmare and Escape from Meridell Castle have avatars associated with them. But these avatars require you to be on the top 50 of the high score list. After scores reset night, the high score list will be at their lowest making it a great opportunity to go for it. You just need to hold your place in the top 50 until 11.50pm. This may be a good opportunity to try for other game avatars as then you may also manage a trophy at the same time though it's difficult.

    Games Room
    « Prev Next »

    03 | Half Price Day

    Half Price Day is the third day of every month. The official Neopets shops price their stock at half-price, and you can haggle down further from there. Speed is of the essence on this day-- even more restockers than usual will flock to the shops to get a better price for the items and will be snapping things up faster than the younger players who tend to hobble into the shops at any ol' time. Kauvara's Magic Shop and the Post Office tend to be the most competitive.

    The Hidden Tower does not reduce its prices on half price day but is affected by a similar event.

    You can use this shop directory (http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=shopsdirectory) to locate the best deals during Half Price day!

    14 | Sloth Day

    Neopia. What a lovely planet. I think I'll take it. – Dr. Frank Sloth

    14th of the Month of Sleeping, Neopets celebrates the Neopian world holiday of Sloth Appreciation Day in honor of the great Dr.Frank Sloth, arch-nemesis of the proud and poised Space Faerie, founder and sole owner of Virtupets Corp. and the most feared and vile villain (despite the absolute delight captured in these post-nuclear takeover photos found on his Internet dating profile) in all of Neopia. though Dr. Sloth is currently floating around in space somewhere, it is implied he will return with new plot to enslave Neopia under his malice rule. Meanwhile what remains of his own personal planet known as the Virtupets Space Station thrives under Neopian rule and together celebrate Dr. Sloth on this day for reasons that are unknown.
    Learn more about Dr. Frank Sloth in this month's feature!

    This month Quirky Aesthetic will be hosting our very own and third annual Sloth Day celebration! Our event staff will be showering players with free themed items in the guild board, hosting giveaways, NC/NP raffles, auctions, board games and more.

    All posting members will receive door prizes, raffle entries, auction access and our featured festival guild badge displayed here so be sure not to miss out on the fun! click here for a complete list of monthly guild badges.

    If you're interested in volunteering for this festival please comment on our festival thread (leadership board) or nm katelynnfitz and we'll provide you with a substantial amount to disperse to fellow participating guild members and an official volunteer guild badge.

    Hidden Tower Discount

    If your account is over 60 months old, you can visit the Hidden Tower on the third Wednesday of each month and the prices are slashed by 3%. This makes a big difference though when buying those really expensive items, with prices reaching in the hundred thousands or even millions of Neo! If you're planning on buying from the HT, it is suggested that you wait until that day to avoid overpaying.

    18 | Deadline Day

    Our many vouchers and prize shoppes introduced from our previously featured month will now expire at the end of the month. However, many events that require end of the month participation such as : kind club, pageant, subscriber's club and more ... will cease sign-ups on the 18th. So be sure to sign up for events and submit your participation info by this date.

    Events such as AI, Game Challenge, Bingo acc.umulate points/participation throughout the month and will be available through the last day of the month.
    « Prev Next »

    Obelisk War

    The Tyrannian Battleground is an ongoing feature in the Battledome where you get to choose a faction to join and fight for every two weeks. At the end of each two week cycle, the Oracle awards prizes to the winning faction.

    The Battleground is a follow-up from the War for the Obelisk event (https://www.jellyneo.net/?go=tyrannia_plot), in which six factions fought over a magical obelisk that appeared in Neopia.

    Sign Ups

    Every other Monday, head on over to the battleground to enlist yourself among the brave warriors. You have three days to sign up with your faction of choice. Each cycle, three random factions will be selected to participate in that week's battle. The prizes you receive (see the Boons section below) differ depending on your faction, so it can be more advantageous to join in depending on the available factions.

    Battling

    The fighting kicks off on the Thursday following sign ups and continues for four days. Your faction leader will help you keep track of your battles during each skirmish. In order to qualify as having helped your faction, you have to take part in at least 10 battles, regardless of difficulty. It is unknown at this time how the difficulty of the challengers affects the number of points your team receives. You can find a list of all the challengers in the JellyNeo In-Depth Battlepedia (http://battlepedia.jellyneo.net/?go=challengers&category=33).

    Prizes: Boons

    If you allied yourself with the victorious faction during a skirmish, then you will be rewarded with your choice of boon (a fancy name for "perks") to enhance the site for the duration of the week-long truce. Each faction has its own list of priorities, so not all boons are available for every faction.

    FULL GUIDE | https://www.jellyneo.net/?go=battleground_of_the_obelisk

    Prize Shoppe Closing

    On the 30th of each month our (NC/NP) vouchers offered from the previous month will officially expire and our prize shop will close, meaning this is the last day to redeem NC or NP prizes from our regional prize shop featured last month. Our new edition of Aesthetic Monthly and it's regionally themed prize shoppe for the month to come are introduced shortly after at the start of the new month. Visit our Prize Shoppe for official information and an active link to last month's issue & prize shoppe. For further details, check out our Index entries on these subjects.

    See our Prize Pool & Prize Pool Index Entry for more details.

    Thank you for your understand and patience with our staff as we conclude our many events hosted each month.

    • Badge & Rank Update
    Upon the conclusion of each month, Quirky Aesthetic Guild Staff Team combine our individual staff logs, databases, post count, member list, recruiting neoboard logging index, official badge log, participation data, activity database and chat notes (notion/alt. chat server) to complete a full Directory update!

    This includes ranks, badges, new directory profile updates and more. Additionally, we will often update staff information, host staff exclusive incentives/raffles/auctions, fill leadership positions and add new staff content at this time or soon after.

    If you have badges that have not yet been logged or maybe you're not sure - you can simply neomail any badge listing to Katelynnfitz or post it to our recruiting neoboard to be logged for the next update. We will check our database and ensure you are logged at that time.

    For more information on Guild Ranks see our webbie pages; where you can also find a complete badge listing.

    You can also refer to our Quirky Guild Index & Reference Guide or more links and information on Quirky Aesthetic membership, promotions, schedules, staff and more.

    This immense update is typically fully complete by the 5th of the following month

    event details

    The Galactic War Pageant

    Choose your Alliance
    Dr. Sloth's remaining force in Virtupets Space Station are awaiting their rulers return and their numbers are growing by the day. Guardian protector of Neopia's outer realm and arch nemesis of Dr. Sloth, the Space Faerie and her Galactic Defense Legion is more prepared than ever to rise against any force that threatens peace on Neopia. All neopets choosing to join Dr. Sloth's minion army in arms against the Galactic Defense Legion will be be subject to less than desirable random events...but we can't do that so we'll just be keeping an eye on you. So which side will you choose?

    Dr. Sloth's Neopia Invasion Force
    • If you think your neopet has what it takes to join the elite forces of Dr. Sloth's malevolent empire, arm your fuzzy friend to the teeth with their battle best. Get your ray guns and set them to mutant in preparation for the return of Dr. Sloth and his next mastermind plan. New recruits will receive premium gear from the Virtupet Corp arsonal at the end of the month for their future service in the name of Dr. Franc Sloth.
    		Space Faerie Galactic Defense Legion
    • Join Mila, defender of the intergalactic Neopia and protector of the outer realm in once again banishing those that would oppose the peace Neopia has found at last. Be prepared to face against the likes of Dr. Sloth and his army if he should be determined to return to Neopia and join his remaining force. For their service, pets will be fitted with proper gear at the end of the month.

    Allegiance to the dominion of the all powerful Dr. Sloth will earn you this badge.

    Pledge to the Space Faerie Galactic Defense Legion to earn this guild badge.

    SPACE ARCADE GAME CHALLENGE

    This month, we invite you to compete against the talented players of Quirky Aesthetic for the top scores in these featured titles of this month's Space Arcade! Record your top scores and game results throughout the month on the survey below and earn raffles, prizes, vouchers and more for participating in this month's Space Arcade selection. Hosted by Katelynnfitz.

    Send scores to our Game Master for each featured game and be included on our scoreboard at the end of the month to earn this guild badge to add to your directory guild profile at the end of the month.

    Alien Aisha Vender Machine

    Play Game | See Rankings
    Put a Nerkmid in the machine, and it will dispense rare and exotic foods for your pet. Press the buttons and push the levers for a chance to get a rarer treat. The better the Nerkmid, the better your prize!

    This arcade feature will award prizes to the playeping the single most valuable reward
  • Rewards for top players, trophies, raffles, AI players and more.
  • http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=alien_aisha_vending_machine

    • Gormball

    Play Game | See Rankings
    Ah, Gormball. That most timeless of Neopian sports, enjoyed by children and adults alike. Two parts hot potato, one part water balloon fight, and with just a dash of alien invasion, it's sure to be unlike any other game you've played before. When Deckball just won't cut it and Wingoball is a little too creepy, it's gotta be Gormball!

    Participants will be ranked according to their top score in this arcade game.
  • Rewards for top players, avatar, trophies, raffles, AI players and more.
  • http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=gormball

    • Neocola Machine

    Play Game | stock tokens
    The Neocola Machine is located on scenic Kreludor, and if you're wondering how it works, you've come to the right place!.
    In order to use the Neocola Machine, you need to obtain one of three Neocola Tokens awarded in the Cosmic Dome or buyable at Space Station Weaponry

    This arcade feature will award prizes to the playeping the single most valuable reward
  • Rewards for top players, trophies, raffles, AI players and more.
  • http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=neocolamachine

    • Caption Contest

    Play Game | See Rankings
    The Caption Contest is regarded as one of the easiest contests on the site. You don't need immense amounts of talent to win this contest, just a good sense of humour. Basically, what you have to do is look at the picture and come up with a funny caption! If your caption is one of the funniest, you win Neopoints, an avatar, and a rare item.

    save any and all captions submitted for your participation survey and include any follow up results from TNT
  • Raffled rewards reserved for Caption Contest participants in addition to special prizes for top/liked captions from our team & site results if caption is accepted for voting.
  • http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=caption_contest

    Galactic Exploration Account Improvement Project

    Since Sloth's defeat, the resistance has been consolidated into the Virtupets Space Station Security Force, or VSSSF for short. This has operatives in a number of different areas, including safety inspectors. There is a comprehensive training manual for safety recruits that includes directives like, "Don't hurt your paw - use a Magnet Claw!", "Ruckuses are unsafe and must not, under any situation, be caused", and "Never look a Money Tree in the mouth, but always approach with hedge clippers!" It has at very least ten sections, each with many subsections of their own. A position of High Blarpxarl can be claimed by successfully removing the Kreludan Blade from a stone on the moon's surface.

    Explore the Neopian Galaxy of dryad planetoids and the dystopian domicile of Dr. Franc Sloth by completing this month's featured regional daily, weekly and bonus challenges to earn points towards our regional/themed prizes in our Stellar Prize Shoppe.Tally your points earned daily on the provided template towards your final score for the month. Account Improvement points earned in this event will be converted to up to 500,000 NP in prize voucher points at the end of the month! Account Improvement is hosted by staff member : Blaz, Classified_Pet.

    POST SCORESHEET SEND FINAL SCORE
    • To begin our Account Improvement Challenge you'll first need to copy our "score-sheet" shown here listing each of our challenges for your records.
    • Carefully read each of our featured challenges and aim to collect upon completing them. for each challenge completed, add a tally to the score to the left of the tag. This represents the number of times you've completed that challenge.
    • Update the sub-totals and totals using the formulas ('#' = times completed, '00' = total in that category, 'x' = multiply, etc.) on your score-sheet and post your updated score-sheet to our recruiting neoboard each week! to report your point values. Scores must be submitted by Saturday @11:58PM to earn for that week!
    • to claim NP: At the end of the month/beginning of the next (25th-5th), send your final AI score-sheet to Classified_Pet to receive Prize Shoppe vouchers for your AI ! (~up to 500K NP)
    • Your NP/vouchers can then be used to purchase items from our Prize Shoppe according to their NP values.
      See Player Records for recent AI Scores and prizes points awarded. (voucher items are not sent for this event, instead the total NP earned will be added directly to your prize point total)

    Moon Rock BINGO

    A meteor crashes onto Kreludor. What do you do? Well, you can do two things. You can either poke it with a stick or just walk away from it. Whatever your choice, collecting items from this mysterious venue will contribute towards your progress in this month's unique Bingo Challenge.

    Unique rules apply to each month's bingo event, please read our instructions carefully:

    how to play

    • Create a gallery category named 'bingo' or clear out last month's category used by the same name.
    • Venture forth to the dryad surface of Kreludor and seek out the mysterious Meteor Crash Site 725-XZ (http://www.jellyneo.net/?go=meteor) for further inspection up to once each hour.
      You have a 25% chance of collecting a item with each inspection
    • Claim up to one new bingo item per day from this venue after any number of visits to the notorious crash site and log new items claimed with the survey provided below.
    • Items won featured on this bingo card should be added to your gallery to show your progress.
    • If you qualify for a bingo after claiming five items in a row as shown on our card, complete the 'claiming bingo' form below and submit it to our emcee.
    Claim Item
    Post Results
    claiming bingo

    Collect any 5 items in a row (in any direction) as shown on the bingo card displayed here to be awarded our bonus prizes; use the survey below to report your bingo to our event host.

    claim bingo
    send bingo

    All users claiming at least one bingo will be awarded this featured 'Moon ROck Bingo Challenge' badge for their guild profile!

    Cosmic Realm Quest

    The Galactic Realm of Neopia consists of two planetoids divided by allegiance, power and history.

    Search the cosmic realm of Neopia for these unique items to redeem for quest prizes

    Find the following items exclusively from any regional venues (update: now obtain items from any official region venue in our lore column) within the vast expansion of the Neopian solar system and redeem them during the month of January for one of our many featured prizes from your Quest Emcee Amonsunamun using the form below.

    By the way, we're not sending you just anywhere! We encourage you to become familiar with these venues as each of them can yield large profits, avatars, high value prizes and more. The shops we ask you to lurk can offer you many of millions (check out our shopping lists for shop inventories and see what items yield extremely high profits in these featured shops and watch for them while you're looking for quest items!) if you catch rare items and the dailies can reward un-buyable items on occasion! Those participating in this event might take interest in collecting AI while searching these locations. See our Account Improvement Challenge above and earn for completing daily activities, challenges and more.

    Contributions

    In recent years, Quirky Aesthetic has grown to support a great variety of activities, events, celebrations and more hosted by our dedicated staff team. As our guild grows, we develop new ways to organize information, communicate, make exchanges and efficiently manage our guildly responsibilities. To better suit our staff's needs, we will now be encouraging pure donations to fund our activities so we can compensate our hosts accordingly and allow them to obtain items based on their needs. We greatly hope you'll continue to offer your support by contributing to our planned activities with the following donation options below. Additionally, we will now be encouraging members to donate themed items directly to hosts within 48 hours of their scheduled volunteer shift to increase their event budget and allow for more festivities. Keep an eye out for our host's announcements posted on our guild board(s) and feel free to lend them your support!

    Purchase scratchcards from our guild shop to offer additional support or visit our Index:Donations on for more information on a variety of accepted donations.

    End of the Year Contest

    Our end of the year contest will challenge participating players of Terror Mountain in a show of community, dedication, festivity and friendship. During our recent updates; we recorded player post counts for the semi-quarter during our last update and will continue to do so, allowing us to track member posts through the end of the year along with our badges earned. Additionally a few other metrics have been added to offer a higher level of competition for those aiming for the one and only grand prize offered for this epic event. This contest has been sponsored by guild staff member, event emcee and prize donor : amonsumamun. Offering our top member declared in the new year the petpet avatar item: Meowclops! unpainted

    Members interested in competing for this grand prize will be required to submit a short survey and a meowclops inspired pet design customization challenge entry featuring one of your pets (however your fashionable design capabilities will lay only a small part in this contest as the nature of this event is to measure your guild spirit and love for our grand community and it's many quirky endeavors) to serve as their leaderboard mascot below (coming soon).

    If you dream of owning a meowclops for your beloved pet and would like to compete with other members in this community challenge please proceed. Once applied, you'll be required to calculate and submit your final score in a simple fashion before January 15th to be considered.

    Scoring & participation

    The following points are awarded to participating members towards a final score that will determine our winner:
    • 1 Pts (each) | Posting | Posts to our private board made 12/01/21 - 01/01/22.
      overposting (back to back) will not be permitted. aka blatant spamming. blah blah rules. father christmas. moving on
    • 10 pts (each) | Badges | Badges earned in our upcoming badge updates (through January).
    • 30 pts (~5 entries) | Design | Awarded to sponsors top favorite customization designs
    • 40 pts (each) | Referral | Mentioned on a member application as the referring member
    enter contest (01/01)
    submit    		finalize score (1/15)

    Welcome to The Galactic Realm of Neopia

    The outter realm surrounding Neopia's moon known as Kreludor homes the Virtupet's Space Station, a large populations of Grundos and allies of Mila the Space Faerie. Visit the locations scattered throughout Neopia's Cosmic Realm in the links provided below:

    Galactic realm Locations

    visit Virtupets Space Stations

    The Virtupets® Orbital Space Station #4 has been the outer space destination of choice since its discovery in Year 2 on the 17th Day of Hiding. It is home to around 1,000 Grundos, and a fair number of other Neopets. It's free to explore, just make sure you stay away from the airlocks!

    Hangar (quadrant)
    Recreations Deck (quadrant)
    Space Weaponry (shop)
    Space Armour (shop)
    Robo Petpets (shop)
    Grundo Cafe (shop)
    Lever of Doom (daily)
    Metoer Crash Site (daily)
    Adopt a Grundo
    Grundo Warehouse
    Nermid Machine (game)
    Gormball (game)
    Cosmic Dome Arena
    visit kreludor

    Kreludor is one of Neopia's moons (other small moons such as Lunaria exist that are not known to many) is also the home of a colony of Grundos. Dr. Sloth is also up to his own nefarious schemes on the surface, but it's still a lovely holiday spot! It was discovered by modern Neopia in Year 6 on the 5th Day of Hunting.

    Booktastic Books (shop)
    Cafe Kreludor (shop)
    Kreludor Mining Corp
    Neocola Machine
    Neocola Centre Arena
    Kreludor Homes (shop)

    Residents of the Galactic Realm

    Cosmic Characters
    • Gorix | Grundo | Neopedia

      Gorix and his brother, Glaxi, were captured by Sloth during his first invasion. Gorix managed to escape, and since then has been fighting in the Resistance. He worked closely with Parlax until the latter betrayed him, although Better Than You #714 implied the pair have somehow reconciled. Gorix had a key role in stopping Sloth's second invasion of the space station.

      Welcome to the Resistance.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/814/)

    • Evil Sloth Clone

      The Evil Sloth Clone is one of the Doctor's many robot incarnations. It guards the mysterious mining facility on Kreludor. Sometimes, a Sloth Clone may go rogue and attack Neopia, similar to what this one did. The Defenders of Neopia were thankfully ready to answer the call! The Sloth clones made a brief appearance in the Return of Dr. Sloth plot, guarding their master onboard his flagship.

      AHHH!!! Yuck another NeoPet!

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/787/)

    • Bernard | Grundo | Booktastic Books

      Bernard runs the Booktastic Book shop on Kreludor, and has his own book club (complete with rewards). He doesn't seem that happy about it though.

      *sigh* you don't really want to buy a book do you? Well... if you like my books that much, I guess you could join the Booktastic Book Club. But only if you want to.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/1470/)

    • Zyrolon | Grundo | Virtupets Resident

      Zyrolon was one of the programmers involved in creating Neopet V2. He has since moved on to repairing the vending machines on the station.

      Even I can't figure out a way to get past all these darn pop-ups, and I'm a programmer! Could you do me a favour and help out with getting rid of them? I'm getting too old to click on them fast enough. I have something for you if you do a stellar job of it. They're only slightly used...

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/736/)

    • Ylana Skyfire | Acara | Neopedia

      his Acara was originally named Ylana Claymore, and born into a life of wealth in a 75 room mansion. When the bank foreclosed on her family's fortune, Ylana ran away from home - cutting all ties. She travelled to the space station where she became a bounty hunter.

      She was hired by Dr. Sloth in an effort to stop the activities of the resistance. Her first mission was to track and detain the Cybunny Scout. However, this took a bit longer than she thought it would. When Dr. Sloth was defeated, Ylana assumed her services were no longer needed, and teleported off the space station.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/851/)

    • Ursula | Usul | Gormball

      Famed to have trained at the top of Mount Usalin, Ursula placed third in the Annual Gormball Championship, Year 2, and managed a first place in Year 4 and Year 12. She is known as a tireless worker who is not only dedicated to the sport, but also to fair play.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/246/)

    • Sophix II | aisha

      This alien Aisha is an agent for Sloth, and works as one of his mercenaries alongside Ylana Skyfire. During the invasion of the space station, Sophix deployed the Grundo Bots to stop the resistance.

      You know, I always wanted to be a singer. I just work for old slime-head to pay the bills.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/864/)

    • Mira, Space Faerie

      Rarely seen in Neopia because she's always soaring across the galaxies, Mira the Space Faerie has protected Neopets from cosmic danger for as long as anyone can remember. Though every now and then she'll visit the planet to task Neopians with her quests, which when completed can raise a Neopet's stats up 4 levels!

      A few years back when the Virtupets Space Station was first introduced, she was the hero of the Virtupets plot and stopped Dr. Sloth from his very first attempt to take over Neopia.

      The Space Faerie has the ability to feel pain when Neopets are in harm's way, and also has the power of telepathy. Whenever she's needed, she'll swoop in to save the day.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/58/)

    • Happiness Faerie

      One of the lesser known Faeries, the Happiness Faerie may be the manifestation of Doctor Sloth's better side, spreading his weird and nerve-wracking happiness to all Neopia. Conquering the world? Nah; it couldn't be further from his mind.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/211/)

    • Gargarox Isafuhlarg | grundo | Neopedia| Cafe| Game

      Gargarox Isafuhlarg is the head chef of Grundo's Cafe, situated at the center of the Virtupets Space Station. But when he isn't busy restocking his shop, he loves to play Gormball. He placed second in the Annual Gormball Championship in Year 4, and third in Years 3 and 6. He also supplies catering for the Championship. He eventually won in Year 11.

      Oops, maybe I should have used a little more Brangerplex

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/242/)

    • Commander Garoo | Blumaroo

      Commander Garoo is one of Doctor Sloth's top subordinates. He's a mean, ruthless Blumaroo that doesn't care much about who or what he has to find, beat or take in order to keep climbing the ladder, really.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/309/)

    • Ace Zafara Advert Attack

      Ace is the star character of Virtupets Studios' latest game: Super Race. Although actually, Super Race is just a game within another game, Advert Attack. In the game you control Ace, racing against the computer-controlled Race Robot to zoom past the finish line first.

      (https://bookofages.jellyneo.net/characters/67/)

    community column

    Here in our Community Column we highlight a select few of the many accomplishments and kind acts of our members in addition to our recent pageant winners and upcoming birthdays. We also encourage our members to share featured members, user shops, pet pages, layouts, nc lists, member goals, collections, portfolio links, customizations, pets, guides, galleries, and more of your own or fellow members of Quirky Aesthetic. If you would like to feature a fellow member or your own highlight here, contact Katelynnfitz. Each time you feature any entry in our monthly publication, you'll earn this month's Aesthetic Monthly badge! User's that are nominated by leadership, members or staff to be in our featured spotlight in this column will receive our new monthly.

    Quirky Clubs

    Click here to visit our new club page by your Club President

    Quirky Clubs offer a unique activities to members seeking assistance in building their collections, trading neocash, training their pets and exploring new site areas.Although we suggest you choose Collections that you are most interested in; as these new collections evolve they will involve more participation for members as they may offer : newsletters, additional badges, contests, giveaways, updates, exclusive auctions, group activities and more. For now, we're simply offering the Collection items and a few perks to be revealed later in the month. To participate in Club Collections, sign up forms MUST be sent by the 18th.

    Quirky Kind Club

    The Quirky Kind Club offers a monthly gift exchange among club members forming a small community from within of those that enjoy spreading kindness, friendship and most of all ... presents! Browse club member collections, profiles, interests, wishlists and more each month and search for the ideal gift to deliver to each of your club-mates for a fun, all-out personal gift-exchange experience that's next level! (kind of like Christmas - no yea... exactly like that but every month!)

    Members participating in this club will send presents to all other club members once per month! There will be no price cap for this activity and members will be encouraged to send gifts as often as they like; however we will send out our newsletter for this club once per month with all club members listed for the official exchange of each month.

    This club is now eligible for auctions, raffles, exclusive games and more! see your club page or president for official details or potential hosting opportunities.

    This badge is awarded to members signing up for NC Closet Club for the first time! Include this badge your active badge log to report.

    Earn our two event badges by participating in this wishing event. Badges displayed here are awarded to wishes and gifting members!. Thank you for playing!

    Taste the Galaxy

    Grundo Smore | AllRecipes

    Chocolate and mallow heated together on delicious Grundo graham cra-ckers.

    Ingredients
    • 1 large marshmallow
    • 1 graham cra-cker
    • 1 (1.5 ounce) bar chocolate candy bar

    Instructions

    • Heat the marshmallow over an open flame until it begins to brown and melt.
    • step two
    • Break the graham cra-cker in half. Sandwich the chocolate between the cra-cker and the hot marshmallow. Allow the marshmallow to cool a moment before eating.

    Kreludor Cake Pops | AllRecipes

    looks just like Kreludor, dont it?
    Create these chocolate cake pops and decorate them to resemble your favorite dark moon.

    Ingredients
    • 1 (15.25 ounce) package chocolate or choice cake mix (such as Betty Crocker®)
    • 1 cup water
    • 3 eggs
    • ½ cup vegetable oil
    • 1 (8 ounce) package cream cheese, softened
    • lollipop sticks
    • 1 (14 ounce) bag chocolate confectioners' coating

    Instructions

    • Preheat oven to 350 degrees F (175 degrees C). Grease a 9x13-inch baking dish.
    • Beat cake mix, water, eggs, and vegetable oil together in a bowl using an electric mixer on low speed for 30 seconds; increase speed to medium and beat until batter is smooth, about 2 minutes more. Pour batter into the prepared baking dish.
    • Bake in the preheated oven until a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, 28 to 33 minutes. Cool cake completely, at least 1 hour.
    • Crumble cake into a large bowl and mix in cream cheese. Roll cake mixture into about 40 to 50 quarter-size bal.ls. Insert a lollipop stick into each cake ball and arrange on a baking sheet; refrigerate until chilled, at least 30 minutes.
    • Melt chocolate in a microwave-safe glass or ceramic bowl in 15-second intervals, stirring after each melting, 1 to 3 minutes.
    • Dip each cake ball into melted chocolate until coated. Arrange cake pops on a baking sheet to dry.

    You can use different food coloring for the chocolate. White chocolate bark or almond bark (inexpensive and can be used in combination with white chocolate) can be used in place of the chocolate bark, if desired.

    Add coloring to the icing to create various colors as well as sprinkles and fun decorations to your cake pops to match any theme. Various cake flavors can also be used, specifically yellow for easy to color mix.

    Sloth Cone | AllRecipes

    Bow down to this mighty Sloth Cone before it melts.

    This is a simple way to make ice cream with three ingredients. Pistachio is my favorite flavor, but any pudding flavor will do. I used skim milk with great results but am certain that fuller fat milk would result in an even creamier product.

    Ingredients
    • 1 (14 ounce) can sweetened condensed milk
    • 1½ cups milk
    • 1 (3.4 ounce) package instant pistachio pudding mix
    • Ice Cream Cones (optional)

    Instructions

    • Mix sweetened condensed milk, milk, and pudding mix together in a bowl; transfer to an ice cream maker and process according to manufacturers' instructions.
    • Once finished, scoop into cone and shape into an ugly Sloth head for best results.

    taste of Christmas

    Winter Snowflake Cake | wilton

    Bake up a blizzard with this Winter Wonderland Snowflake Cake. Iced in light blue icing, then decorated with sprinkles and icing decorations, this winter-themed cake is perfect for a winter birthday or Hanukkah celebration. Use a cookie cutter and nonpareils to create a fun decoration on the top of the cake that gives this dessert that little touch of something extra without any hard work! -wiltonrecipes Ingredients
    • Favorite Cake Mix or Recipe
    • Creamy White Decorator Icing, 4 lb. Tub
    • Royal Blue Icing Color, 1 oz. - Blue Food Coloring
    • Snowflake Icing Decorations
    • Assorted sprinkles
    Tools
    • Non-Stick Cooling Grid - 14.5 x 20-Inch - Cooling Rack
    • Decorating Bags, 16-Inch Disposable Piping Bags, 12-Count
    • Decorator Preferred Round Cake Pan, 8 x 3-Inch
    • Straight Icing Spatula, 11-Inch - Straight Cake Spatula
    • tweezers
    • Open Star Cake Decorating Tip 21
    • Snowflake Cookie Cutter Set, 3-Piece

    Instructions

    • Bake cake. Prepare cake batter following recipe instructions. Bake and cool two cake layers. Trim each layer to 2½ in. tall. Assemble for 5 in. tall cake.
    • Tint icing. Using Royal Blue icing color, tint 4 cups icing pale blue. Using spatula, ice cake, leaving horizonal spatula marks on sides of cake and swirl on top of cake.
    • Mix sprinkles. Mix 6-cell sprinkles together. With hand, carefully press sprinkles mix along bottom of cake. For best results, do this over a large pan or dish to catch excess sprinkles.
    • Make snowflake. Place snowflake cutter on top of cake. Fill with thin layer of white nonpareils. Carefully remove cutter. Using tweezers, remove any nonpareils, if needed.
    • Decorate cake. Prepare decorating bag with tip 21 and creamy white icing. Pipe small swirls around top of cake. Top each swirl with snowflake icing decoration.

    Snow Faerie Puffs | SizzlingEats

    This easy cream puff recipe uses simple ingredients and only takes 20 minutes to make! The flaky puff pastry crust and real cream filling make these cream puffs a perfect party dessert! Ingredients
    • 1 box Puff Pastry Sheets
    • 1-pint heavy whipping cream
    • 1 tsp vanilla extract
    • 1/4 cup confectionery sugar
    Utensils
    • Cookie Cutter (I used snowflake shapes, but you can use whatever shape you want.)
    • Baking Sheet
    • Oven
    • Electric hand or stand mixer

    Instructions

    Shell Instructions
    • Pre-heat oven to 350 degrees.
    • Roll out slightly thawed and pliable puff pastry dough.
    • Carefully cut out the puff pastry shapes and place them on a large baking sheet that's lined with parchment paper.
    • Once all puff pastry shapes are cut out, re-roll the dough and cut out more if needed.
    • Place in oven on center rack. Bake 10-12 mins
    • Remove from oven. Allow to cool for 1-2 minutes.
    • Using a bread knife, carefully slice the puff pastry in half.
    Filling Instructions
    • Add all heavy whipping cream, vanilla extract, and confectioners sugar ingredients to a large bowl.
    • Beat on high until peaks form and remain steady.
    • Add the filling to a pastry bag and pipe into each snowflake. You can also just spoon it onto the pastry.
    chef's notes
    • Use chilled puff pastry dough and cut it on a floured surface.
    • When mixing the whipped cream filling, use a chilled bowl and cold cream.
    • Keep the whipped cream filling chilled when it’s not in use.
    nutrition
      Serving: 1cream puff | Calories: 223cal | Carbohydrates: 13g | Protein: 2g | Fat: 18g | Saturated Fat: 7g | Cholesterol: 32mg | Sodium: 70mg | Potassium: 32mg | Sugar: 1g | Vitamin A: 350IU | Vitamin C: 0.2mg | Calcium: 18mg | Iron: 0.6mg

    Cake Batter Slushie | NoviceChef

    This cake batter milkshake recipe is so delicious and easy to make. just toss all the ingredients in a blender and you’ll have a homemade milkshake in less than 5 minutes! Ingredients
    • 4 large scoops Vanilla ice cream
    • 1/2 cup yellow cake mix
    • splash of milk sprinkles for garnish

    Instructions

    • In a blender, combine all ingredients (except for sprinkles). Blend until well combined, serve immediately.
    • For sprinkle edges: rub a thin layer of corn syrup on the rim of your glass and dip in colorful sprinkles!
    nutrition

    Molten Hot Chocolate | thebanditrocks
    Ingredients

    • Paint Pens
    • 1 packet hot Chocolate
    • 1 cup whole milk
    • Mini marshmallows

    Instructions

    • Clean your mug and dry it completely before starting. Use your paint pens to draw any design you would like on your mug! Let dry overnight.

    Lava Chilaquiles | thebanditrocks
    IngredientsFor Tortilla Chips*:
    • 12 6” corn tortillas
    • 2 quarts vegetable oil
    • Kosher salt
      • For Salsa Roja:
    • 1.5 lbs. tomatoes
    • ½ large yellow onion--
    • 1 medium jalapeno
    • 2 cloves garlic
    • 1 c chicken broth
    • 2 tsp vegetable oil
    • Kosher salt, to taste
    For Fried Eggs:
    • 2 eggs
    • 3 Tbsp. butter
    • Optional Garnishes:
    • Diced Avocado
    • Mexican Crema
    • Queso Fresco

    Instructions

    Make the Salsa Roja:
    • Roughly cut the yellow onion_ core and quarter the tomatoes, remove the seeds and membrane from the jalapeno, and peel the garlic cloves. Toss all ingredients into a blender or food processor and blend until completely smooth. Add the chicken broth and blend well.
    • Heat the oil in a large sk1llet over medium heat. Add the blended mixture and cook over medium-low heat until thickened (about 15-20 minutes).
    • While the salsa simmers, prepare the tortilla chips.
    Make the Tortilla Chips:
    • Heat the oil in a deep fryer. Cut the tortillas into 6 pieces.
    • Working in batches, deep fry the tortillas for about 1 minute, or until they start to brown on the edges. Be sure to shake the basket to prevent the chips from sticking to each other. Remove the chips to a paper-towel lined plate and sprinkle with salt.
    Make Fried Eggs and Assemble Chilaquiles:
    • In a small, nonstick sauté pan, melt the butter. Carefully c.rack eggs into the pan and let fry for 1-2 minutes. If you're brave, or if you prefer your eggs cooked on both sides, flip and cook for a few seconds (no more than 20, or the yolk will start to set).
    • Place the tortilla chips into the large pan with the salsa roja, and very carefully toss until they are completely coated.
    • Remove chilaquiles to a large serving platter – top with fried egg and any optional toppings you may want!
    Notes:
    • You can use store-bought tortilla chips instead of making your own!

    Lemon Lava Cake | thebanditrocks
    IngredientsFor Lava Cake
    • 2 oz white Chocolate baking bar
    • ¼ c unsalted butter
    • 1/3 c all-purpose flour
    • ¼ c powdered sugar
    • 1/8 tsp salt
    • 2 large eggs
    • 2 large egg yolks
    • 1/3 c lemon curd
    • 3 tsp fresh lemon zest
    • ¼ tsp vanilla extract
    For Topping
    • ½ c heavy cream
    • 1 ½ Tbsp powdered sugar
    • Raspberries
    • Blueberries

    Instructions

    • Preheat the oven to 425°F. Place three glass or ceramic ramekins on a rimmed baking sheet, and spray with nonstick cooking spray.
    • Melt the butter and Chocolate in a microwave safe bowl. Microwave in short bursts (start with 30 seconds) and stir well. If more microwaving is needed, microwave for 10 seconds then stir well.
    • To the bowl, add the flour, powdered sugar, and eggs. Whisk to combine. Then add the eggs, egg yolks, lemon curd, lemon zest and vanilla extract. Whisk well to combine.
    • Add ½ cup to each ramekin and bake for 12-15 minutes – the edges should be golden brown, but the middle of the cake should NOT be set (this is what makes the lava in the lava cake!)
    • Let cool on a wire rack for 10 minutes before serving. Meanwhile, whip the cream with the powdered sugar until stiff peaks form.
    • Plate the lava cake with the whipped cream and fresh berries, and enjoy!

    Molten Candy Apple | 'Nerdy Mamma'

    Ingredients
    • 1 dozen small Apples at room temperature
    • 1 dozen Lollipop Sticks or cut and cleaned twigs
    • 3 cups granulated Sugar
    • 3 / 4 cup Light Corn Syrup
    • 1-1/2 cups Water
    • 3 / 4 cup Cinnamon Imperial Candies
    • 1-1/2 teaspoons Ground Cinnamon
    • 3 / 4 teaspoon Red Food Color

    Instructions

    • Wash the room temperature apples, remove the stems, and place on paper towels to drain.
    • Cover a large baking sheet with wax paper and coat the paper with cooking spray.
    • Using a soft cloth or paper towel, completely dry the apples (this step is very important). If the apples are not dry, the hot candy may splatter when the apple is inserted in it.
    • Place a Lollipop Stick or Twig into the stem end of each apple, pushing each about halfway through the apple.
    • Combine the granulated Sugar and Cinnamon in a medium saucepan.
    • Add the Corn Syrup, Water, Cinnamon Imperials, and Vanilla. Place over medium heat and stir continually until the sugar is dissolved.
    • Clip a candy thermometer to the saucepan, bring the mixture to a boil and continue to stir frequently until all the candies are dissolved and the mixture reaches 285⁰.
    • Remove from heat and let the mixture sit for about a minute until some of the bubbles have dissipated.
    • Working quickly, dip each apple into the hot syrup and spin to coat.
    • Withdraw the apple and continue to hold over the saucepan to let some of the syrup drip back into the pan. Move the coated apple to the was-paper covered baking sheet.
    • Allow the apples to cool to room temperature.
    • Place in an airtight container to store for a couple of days only.

    Boiling Hot Lava Soup | Yummy Yoo-Hoo!

    These thick noodles make a great and filling lunch or dinner. (2,550 NP) Ingredients
    • 1 onion_ white)
    • 2 carrots
    • 4 tablespoons olive oil
    • 2 garlic cloves (peeled and crushed)
    • 2 tablespoons flour
    • 1 (28 ounce) can chopped tomatoes
    • 2 tablespoons tomato paste
    • 2 teaspoons fresh thyme leaves
    • 4 cups vegetable (or chicken) stock
    • 2 pinches sugar
    • 2 squeezes of lemon juice
    • Ground black pepper

    Instructions

    • Peel and dice the onion and carrot. Heat the oil in a medium saucepan over medium heat.
    • Add the onion and carrot to the pan and cook them for about 5 minutes to soften, stirring occasionally. Stir in the garlic and the flour and cook the mixture for 1 minute.
    • Add the tomatoes, tomato paste, stock, sugar, and lemon juice and bring to a boil. Reduce to a simmer and cook for 20 – 25 minutes. Take the soup off the heat and leave it to cool.
    • Ladle the soup into a blender, season with pepper, and blend until smooth. Pour the soup back into the pan and bring to a simmer.
    • Ladle the soup into bowls and serve with warm, toasted bread.

    Fire Rice | Food/lauralie41

    Not only is this rice spicy, it is also aflame! (1,500 NP) Ingredients
    • 2 2⁄3 cups water
    • 1 1⁄3 cups long grain white rice, uncooked
    • 1lb ground pork breakfast sausage
    • 1 (16 ounce) jar picante sauce
    • 1 (8 ounce) container sour cream
    • 8 ounces cheddar cheese, shredded

    Instructions

    • Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.
    • Bring water to boil in a medium saucepan. Stir in the rice, reduce heat, cover, and simmer for approximately 20 minutes.
    • In a large sk1llet over medium heat brown sausage until no longer pink.
    • In a medium mixing bowl add cooked rice, cooked sausage, picante sauce, and sour cream. Mix well, place in casserole dish, and top with cheddar cheese.
    • Bake approximately 20 minutes or until cheese is bubbly. Serve with sides of extra picante sauce and sour cream.

    Mummy's Meatloaf | dcexpress

    Just don't chew it too fast! Your teeth might melt. Ingredients
    • 1 kg (2 lb.) ground beef
    • 1 onion_ grated,
    • 1 egg
    • 2 tablespoons breadcrumbs
    • 2 cloves of garlic
    • 1 sprig of rosemary, leaves chopped
    • salt & pepper
    Mummification:
    • ketchup mixed with hot hot sauce
    • 2 yellow tomatoes (eyes)
    • blanched almonds
    • 1 package bacon

    Instructions

    • Preheat oven to 400℉ (200℃).
    • Mix the meats with the rest of the ingredients. Form a round loaf with indents for eyes and an open mouth in an ovenproof pan. Place the almonds like teeth in the mouth. Brush the loaf with ketchup mixture. Wrap the bacon around the meatloaf. Use yellow tomatoes for eyes.
    • Cook the meatloaf in the oven for about 20 minutes. Add about a cup of warm water to the pan, this will later be used for the sauce. Cook for 10-15 minutes more until it reaches a center temperature of about 167℉ (75℃).
    The cremated halloween meatloaf
    • Pour the pan drippings into a sauce pan and heat it. Add milk and red currant jelly and thicken the sauce with milk and flour. Season with red currant jelly and salt.
    • Serve the meatloaf with mashed potatoes.

    taste of Halloween

    Monster Cake

    Eat it before it eats you!

    Cook: 3 hr 35 min | Prep: 30 min | Servings: 8-10     Cake Ingredients
    • 2/3 cup vegetable oil, plus more for greasing the baking pans
    • 1 cup Dutch-process cocoa powder
    • 1 cup boiling water
    • 2 cups granulated sugar
    • 1 3/4 cups all-purpose flour (see Cook's Note)
    • 2 teaspoons baking powder
    • 1 teaspoon fine salt
    • 1 cup whole milk
    • 2 large eggs
    • 1 tablespoon pure vanilla extract
    • two 9-inch round cake pans
    Filling and Frosting Ingredients
    • 1 1/2 cups heavy cream
    • 3/4 cup Dutch-process cocoa powder, sifted
    • 8 ounces semisweet chocolate, chopped
    • 1 teaspoon espresso powder
    • 1 teaspoon pure vanilla extract
    • Pinch fine salt
    • 2 tablespoons unsalted butter
    • 1/3 cup confectioners' sugar, sifted
    • (optionally) food coloring for icing
    Monster Eyes
    • 2 Marshmallows (eyes)
    • Cooking Spray
    • Candy Spiders, worms or preferred candy decorations

    Instructions

    • For the cake: Position an oven rack in the center of the oven and preheat to 350 degrees F. Line the bottom of two 9-inch round cake pans with parchment and grease the parchment and the sides of the pans with oil.
    • Stir together the cocoa powder and boiling water in a small bowl and let sit to bloom for 5 minutes (this step intensifies the chocolate flavor in the cake).
    • Whisk together the granulated sugar, flour, baking powder and salt in a large bowl. Whisk together the bloomed cocoa, oil, milk, eggs and vanilla in a medium bowl. Pour the cocoa mixture into the sugar mixture and stir until smooth (the batter will be thin). Divide the batter evenly between the prepared cake pans. Bake until the cakes bounce back when pressed in the middle and a toothpick inserted in the center comes out clean, 30 to 40 minutes. Let cool completely in the pans on a rack.
    • For the filling and frosting: Heat the cream in a double boiler over low heat, whisking occasionally, until it begins to steam. Whisk in the cocoa powder, chocolate, espresso powder, vanilla and salt until the mixture is smooth, about 2 minutes. Whisk in the butter until melted. Whisk in the confectioners' sugar until incorporated. Let the frosting cool completely. (add food coloring for desired color)
    • To assemble: Put 1 cake, bottom-side up, on a serving plate or cake stand. Spread about 1 cup of the frosting over the top but not all the way down the side. Top with the other cake, bottom-side up, and frost the top and sides with the remaining frosting.
    • For the monster decoration: Microwave the marshmallows in a microwave-safe medium bowl until they swell and are soft enough to stir, about 1 minute. Let sit a few minutes until cool enough to touch. Spray your hands with cooking spray. For a spider web, pick up a tablespoon-sized blob of the melted marshmallow and stretch it over and around the cake; repeat so that the strings of marshmallow crisscross one another in many directions, and continue until you have what looks like a spider web. Add two marshmallows for the eyes (dab chocolate for pupils), Garnish with a candy spiders or preferred finishes..

      • Chef's Notes

      The candy decorations are a nice touch, but the cake will be fun and delicious without them as well. When measuring flour, we spoon it into a dry measuring cup and level off the excess. (Scooping directly from the bag compacts the flour, resulting in dry baked goods.)

    Pumpkin Ice Cream

    All the dreamy ingredients of pumpkin pie (even the crust!) are frozen into an ultra-creamy ice-cream treat that doesn't require an ice cream maker or any churning.
    If you are really lucky your ice cream may have some seeds in it.

    Time: 3hr 45min | Serves: 6-8 | Prep: 15min     Ingredients
    • 1 store-bought frozen pie shell
    • 1 teaspoon granulated sugar
    • 1/4 teaspoon ground cinnamon
    • One 15-ounce can pumpkin pie filling
    • One 14-ounce can sweetened condensed milk (about 1 cup)
    • Pinch fine salt
    • 2 cups cold heavy cream
    • Caramel sauce, for drizzling

    Instructions

    • Put a 9-by-5-by-3-inch loaf pan in the freezer to chill. Preheat the oven to 375 degrees F. Sprinkle the pie shell with the sugar and cinnamon and bake until the crust is golden brown, 12 to 14 minutes. Set aside to cool, then crumble.
    • Meanwhile, whisk together the pumpkin pie filling, condensed milk and salt in a large bowl and set aside.
    • Whip the cream with an electric mixer on medium-high until firm peaks form, about 2 minutes. Fold 1 cup of the whipped cream into the condensed milk mixture with a rubber spatula until combined, then fold the lightened mixture into the whipped cream until well blended. Pour half of the ice cream into the chilled loaf pan and layer all but 1 cup of the pie crust over it. Top with the remaining ice cream. Cover with plastic wrap and freeze until solid and scoopable, about 3 hours or up to overnight. Serve with a drizzle of caramel sauce and the reserved pie crust.
    Brought to you by the FoodNetwork: No-Churn Pumpkin Pie Ice Cream

    Pumpkin Cinnamon Yurble Ear

    Yurble ears never tasted so good! It is just dough and pumpkin, thank goodness.

    Tota: 3hr | Yields: 24 Servings | Prep: 1hr     Dough Ingredients
    • 1 1/2 cups whole milk
    • 1/2 cup vegetable oil
    • 1/2 cup granulated sugar
    • 1 package (2 1/4 teaspoons) active dry yeast
    • 1 cup pumpkin puree
    • 4 1/2 cups all-purpose flour, plus more for flouring, sprinkling and rolling
    • 1/2 teaspoon ground cinnamon
    • 1/4 teaspoon ground ginger
    • 1/4 teaspoon ground nutmeg
    • 1/2 teaspoon (heaping) baking powder
    • 1/2 teaspoon baking soda
    • 1/2 teaspoon salt
    • Melted butter, for buttering pans
    Filling Ingredients
    • 1 stick (1/2 cup) butter, melted
    • 1/2 cup brown sugar
    • 1/2 cup granulated sugar
    • 1/2 teaspoon cinnamon
    • 1/2 teaspoon ground ginger
    • 1/4 teaspoon ground nutmeg
    • 1 cup finely chopped pecans
    Frosting Ingredients
    • 8 ounces cream cheese, softened
    • 1 3/4 cups to 2 cups powdered sugar
    • 1/4 cup whole milk, plus more if needed
    • 2 tablespoons butter, melted
    • Dash of salt

    Instructions

    • For the dough: In a large saucepan, combine the milk, vegetable oil and granulated sugar. Heat until hot but not boiling, then remove the pan from the stove and allow it to cool until the mixture is warm to the touch but not too hot. Sprinkle the yeast over the surface of the liquid and allow it to sit for 5 minutes. Stir in the pumpkin puree until combined.
    • Combine 4 cups of the flour with the cinnamon, ginger and nutmeg. Sprinkle it into the saucepan and stir until it just comes together. Cover the saucepan with a dish towel and set in a warm, draft-free place for 1 hour.
    • After 1 hour, the mixture should be very puffy and at least doubled in size. Stir in the baking powder, baking soda, salt and remaining 1/2 cup flour until totally combined.
    • Preheat the oven to 375 degrees F. Drizzle butter into 3 pie pans (or a larger baking dish) and smear it all over the bottom of the pans.
    • For the filling: Drizzle the melted butter over the dough and smear it all over the surface with your fingers. Mix together the brown sugar, granulated sugar, cinnamon, ginger and nutmeg in a medium bowl. Sprinkle this mixture all over the surface of the dough, covering all the melted butter. Sprinkle with 1/2 cup to 3/4 cup chopped pecans
    • Starting at the top, roll the dough toward you into a large log, moving back and forth down the line of dough (in a "typewriter" motion) and always rolling toward you. Roll it tightly as you go so the rolls with be nice and neat. When it's all rolled, pinch the seam closed and turn the roll over so that the seam is facing down. Slice into 1/2- to 3/4-inch slices and place the slices in the buttered pan(s). Allow to rise for 20 minutes.
    • Bake until the rolls are nice and golden brown around the edges, 15 to 18 minutes.
    • For the frosting: While the rolls are baking, make the frosting by combining the cream cheese, powdered sugar, milk, butter and salt in the bowl of an electric mixer. Beat until fluffy, adding more milk if you'd like a thinner frosting.
    • Frost the rolls the second they come out of the oven. Sprinkle the extra pecans over the frosting, then allow them to sit for 15 minutes before serving.
    • Delicious!

    Credit: Pumpkin Cinnamon Rolls by Ree Drummond on Food Network

    Alternatively use the magic cooking pot to create this menacing elixir by combining Brain Tree Root and Eyeb4ll Slushie.

    Lemon Iced Tea | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    Enjoy this famously refreshing beverage on any hot summer day in the desert! (or anywhere else...) Ingredients
    • 2 Lipton Iced Tea Bags (see notes)
    • ¼ c granulated sugar
    • 1 lemon, cut into wedges
    • 4 Cups Water

    Instructions

    • Bring water to a boil. Once boiling, remove from heat, drop in tea bags, and let steep for 10 minutes.
    • After 10 minutes, remove and discard tea bags. Stir in the sugar (you can adjust to taste) and allow to cool to room temperature.
    • After cooling, transfer to a pitcher and place in the fridge to cool completely.
    • After a few hours of chilling, enjoy your tea over ice, with a squeeze of fresh lemon juice.
    • Tea will remain fresh in the fridge for about a week before it will start to sour, so don’t let it linger!
    Notes: For all our international guild members, “Iced Tea” bags are a special, specific thing. Don’t use just any tea bags to make this! Lipton is the best known brand here in the US. Their “Iced Tea” branded tea bags are significantly larger than standard tea bags. If you can’t find the “Iced Tea” bags, use 4 regular-sized Lipton brand tea bags instead.

    Blueberry Moon Tart | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    Over the moon for this epic blueberry tart! (crust) Ingredients
    • 2.5 cups all-purpose flour
    • 6 Tbsp sugar
    • ½ tsp salt
    • 2 sticks (1 cup) unsalted butter, cut into ½ inch cubes
    • 2 large egg yolks
    • 2 Tbsp whipping cream
    (filling) Ingredients
    • ½ cup whipping cream
    • 2 Tbsp cornstarch
    • 2 large eggs
    • 4 large egg yolks
    • 1 tsp vanilla extract
    • ½ cup white balsamic vinegar
    • ¾ cup water
    • ¾ cup sugar
    • ½ stick (1/4 cup) unsalted butter
    (topping) Ingredients
    • 1 pint fresh blueberries
    • 1 cup unsweetened coconut flakes

    (Crust) Instructions

    • In a food processor, combine the flour, sugar and salt and pulse briefly to combine. Add the cubes of butter and pulse to blend until a coarse meal forms. Add egg yolks and whipping cream. Pulse until clumps begin to form. Remove from food processor, and use your hands to work the dough into a b4ll.
    • Press dough into a 9” diameter tart pan with removable bottom. The crust layer should be no more than ¼” thick. Be sure to press the dough up the sides of the pan, too. Peirce dough all over with a fork. Move to fridge and chill for one hour.
    • Preheat the oven to 375 °F. Line the tart with parchment and fill with pie weights (rice or dry beans work if you don’t have ceramic pie weights). Bake until the crust is golden, about 22 minutes. Once baked, cool completely.

    (Filling) Instructions

    • In a large bowl, combine whipping cream and cornstarch until the cornstarch is dissolved. Add the eggs, egg yolks, and vanilla, and whisk to blend.
    • In a medium saucepan, boil the white balsamic vinegar until reduced to ¼ cup (about 3 minutes). Add ¾ cup water, sugar, and butter. Stir until butter melts, then return the mixture to a boil. VERY gradually, whisk the vinegar mixture into the egg mixture. If you do this too fast, you could cook the eggs which is not what you want to do! Pour a slow stream of the hot liquid into the egg mixture, and whisk continuously until completely incorporated.
    • Return the mixture back to the saucepan. Whisk until the custard thickens and boils, about 2-3 minutes. Strain into a bowl and cool completely.
    • Spread the custard into the crust, then cover and chill the tart for at least 3 hours or up to 24 hours.

    (Decorating) Instructions

    • First, toast the coconut. Preheat the oven to 325 °F. Spread the coconut in a thin layer on a baking sheet, and bake for 5-10 minutes, stirring once halfway through. Keep a close eye on your coconut, as once the browning process begins, it happens fast! Cool toasted coconut completely before using.
    • Decorate the tart with blueberries arranged in a crescent moon shape, then add the toasted coconut to the center of the tart. Viola, a fancy and delicious Blueberry Moon Tart!

    Notes from the Chef:

    • Recipe originally from Epicurious. No changes made, other than adding some instructions and doubling the crust recipe because I felt that the original was not enough to cover the entire tart.

    Loveberry Chocolate Mousse | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    Fall in love with this sweet dish! Loveberry” Layer
    • 1 3oz packet strawberry Jell-O powder
    • 1 cup boiling water
    • 2 cups cold water
    Chocolate Mousse Layer
    • ½ cup half and half
    • 2 packets unflavored gelatin
    • 2 cups cold water
    • ½ cup unsweetened cocoa powder
    • 2/3 cup sugar
    To Serve
    • Fresh Strawberries (optional)
    • Fresh Mint (optional)

    “Loveberry” Layer Instructions

    • Place a muffin tin on a flat work surface. Set 6 glasses (12 oz each) on a diagonal in each of the muffin cups and set aside.
    • In a medium bowl, mix boiling water and Jell-O and stir slowly until dissolved. Stir in 2 cups cold water, then set aside to cool.
    • Once the mixture is lukewarm, pour into each glass until you’ve reached ½” below the rim.
    • Keeping the glasses in position, transfer the tray to the fridge to chill for at least 2 hours, or until set. If the glasses are not stable, you can put paper towels below them to keep them from moving so much.

    Chocolate Mousse Layer Instructions

    • In a medium saucepan, add half and half. Sprinkle gelatin on top and set aside for 2 minutes.
    • Whisk in cold water until mixed, then add the cocoa and sugar.
    • Place over medium heat and heat until barely boiling, stirring constantly. Then remove from heat and set aside to cool.
    • When the chocolate mixture is lukewarm, pour into the glasses on top of the set Loveberry layer. *make sure the Jell-O layer is completely set before attempting this, or else the two will mix!*
    • Return the glasses to the fridge and chill for at least one more hour to set.
    • Garnish with a fresh Loveberry (strawberry) and a mint sprig, and enjoy!
    Chef (Erica) Notes: Recipe originally from TipBuzz. No changes made other than the elimination of fresh strawberry within the Jell-O layer, and the garnish.

    Courgette Bread (AKA Zucchini Bread) | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    The fresh baked bread you need in your life right meow! Ingredients
    • 3 large eggs
    • 1 cup vegetable oil
    • 2 cups sugar
    • 3 teaspoons vanilla extract
    • 2 medium or 1 large zucchini
    • 3 cups flour
    • 2 teaspoons cinnamon
    • 1 teaspoon salt
    • 1 teaspoon baking soda
    • 1 teaspoon baking powder

    Instructions

    • Preheat oven to 350° F. Prepare two bread tins by spraying them with non-stick spray and lining them with parchment paper.
    • Beat the eggs in a large bowl, then add the oil, sugar, and vanilla.
    • Use a medium grate to shred the zucchini. Two cups is roughly one large or two medium zucchini. Do not pat the zucchini dry or otherwise attempt to remove the moisture. Add directly to the wet ingredients, and stir to combine.
    • In a medium bowl, combine flour, cinnamon, salt, baking soda and baking powder. Whisk with a fork to combine.
    • In two or three additions, add the flour mixture to the wet ingredients. Mix by hand or with your favorite mixer until there are no more visible lumps of flour in the batter. This will only take a few minutes.
    • Pour the batter into the two prepared bread pans, and bake for 45-60 minutes. I recommend setting a timer for 40 minutes, then checking doneness with a toothpick at 5 minute intervals. The bread is done when a toothpick inserted into the middle of the loaf comes out clean.
    • Remove from pans and allow to cool on wire racks. When cooled, slice and enjoy warm, either plain or with butter!
    • When wrapped in aluminum foil or kept in an airtight container, loaves will keep at room temperature for about a week. Perfect for a busy morning breakfast!
    Chef (Erica) Notes: Y’all, don’t sleep on this recipe. This is my family’s zucchini bread recipe, and it is the simplest and best thing I make. It is my go-to, my comfort food, my all-time favorite, my know-it-by-heart recipe. I hope, of all the recipes I’ve shared, this is the one you guys make for real!

    Ham and Custard Croissant | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    open wide and say 'cheese' for this scrumptious sandwich perfect for picnics, packed lunches And more! Ingredients

    • 1 slice deli ham

    • Top with ham and the top of the croissant, then enjoy!

But if you want to keep this simple breakfast dish easy, grab a fresh croissant from your local bakery!

    Peach Galette | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    This sweet dish with leave you feelin' peachy! Pastry Ingredients
    • ¾ cup All-purpose flour, plus more for dusting
    • 6 Tbsp whole wheat flour
    • 1 Tbsp sugar
    • ½ tsp kosher salt
    • ½ cup + 1 Tbsp unsalted butter, cold and cut into cubes
    • 1 large egg
    • 1.5 tsp milk
    • 1 Tbsp beaten egg or heavy cream
    • Turbinado sugar, for sprinkling (optional)
    Filling Ingredients
    • ½ cup sugar
    • 3 Tbsp all-purpose flour
    • ½ tsp cinnamon
    • 6-8 soft peaches, peeled, halved, pitted and cut into wedges

    Instructions

    • 1) Make the pastry: Combine the flours, sugar, and salt in a food processor and pulse until blended. Add in the butter cubes and pulse until the mixture looks like sand. In a small bowl or cup, whisk together the egg and milk until blended, then pour into the food processor and pulse until the dough just forms a clump. Do not overwork the dough, or it will get tough.
    • Flour your work surface, and turn the dough out onto the surface. Form into a b4ll, then flatten into a disk 1” thick. Wrap in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 2 hours, or up to 1 day.
    • When the dough is chilled, preheat oven to 375°F.
    • Prepare the peaches by stirring together the flour, sugar and cinnamon. Place the sliced peaches in a bowl and sprinkle the sugar mixture over the top, then toss gently to combine. Set aside while you work the dough.
    • Take the dough out of the fridge and let rest for about 10 minutes. Then, on a floured sheet of parchment paper, roll the dough into a circle about 11 inches in diameter and 1/8 inch thick. Transfer the dough and the parchment paper to a rimmed baking sheet.
    • Starting 1.5 inches from the edge of the pastry, place the peach wedges in a single layer, working your way around the edge of the pastry then in towards the center. Once all peaches are placed, fold up the 1.5” edge around the peaches and crimp into place. Brush the pastry border with the beaten egg or heavy cream (your choice) and sprinkle with turbinado sugar.
    • Bake for 50-60 minutes, until the crust is golden and the filling is bubbling.
    • Let the galette cool slightly before slicing into wedges and serving, maybe with some vanilla ice cream on the side!

    Kite Cookies | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    These cookies will have you flying high. (cookies) Ingredients
    • ½ cup (1 stick) unsalted butter
    • ½ cup sugar
    • ¼ cup light brown sugar
    • 1 Tbsp molasses
    • ½ tsp vanilla extract
    • 1 large egg
    • 2 cups flour
    • ¼ tsp salt
    • ¾ tsp baking powder
    • 20-30 hard candies, such as Life Savers or Jolly Ranchers
    (filling) Ingredients
    • 1 7 oz. tub marshmallow cream
    • 1 cup salted butter, at room temperature
    • 1 tsp vanilla extract
    • 1 lb powdered sugar
    • 2-3 tsp milk or heavy cream

    (cookies) Instructions

    • 1) Preheat the oven to 375 °F. Line two large baking sheets with parchment paper.
    • In a large bowl or stand mixer, beat together butter and sugars until fluffy. Add in the molasses and vanilla extract, then the egg. Beat until light and smooth.
    • In a separate bowl, whisk together the flour, salt, and baking powder, then add the dry ingredients to the wet ingredients and mix until the flour is just incorporated.
    • Flatten the dough into a disk, then wrap in plastic wrap and refrigerate for at least 1 hour or up to two days.
    • While the dough is chilling, unwrap the hard candies and crush with a mallet until they are tiny shards (be sure to separate the candies by color, if you’re using multiple colors)
    • Once the dough has chilled, roll the dough into a sheet about ¼” thick, then cut with cookie cutters. To achieve the kite shape, I used a scallop edge square cutter bent into a diamond shape. For half the cookies, leave them whole. For the other half, use a small knife to cut the “windows” out for the candies.
    • Place the cookies on the prepared baking sheets, about 1” apart. Fill each “window” with hard candy pieces. Try to fill as much of the window as possible without letting any candy overflow onto the top of the cookie.
    • Bake for 9-10 minutes. The candy should be bubbly and the cookies just starting to brown. Remove baking sheets from oven and place on a wire rack to cool. Allow cookies to cool completely before removing them from the parchment paper.

    (filling) Instructions

    • Whip the marshmallow cream, butter, and vanilla on medium speed until well combined and fluffy. Add 2 tsp milk or cream plus the powdered sugar, then continue mixing on medium speed until smooth. Add more milk or cream (1/2 tsp at a time) if necessary until desired consistency is reached.

    (preparation) Instructions

    • 1) Place the whole cookies face down on a tray, then pipe the frosting on top. Top with a window cookie and serve!
    Chef (Erica) Notes: cookie recipe originally from Simply Recipes. Frosting Recipe originally from South your Mouth. No changes made to either recipe. If you really want to make these for consumption, please let me recommend you NOT make stained glass window cookies. Instead of filling the windows with hard candies, wait for the cookies to bake, assemble, then fill the windows with strawberry or raspberry jam. Trust me, it will be a much more enjoyable eating experience!

    Lemon Cupcake | Thebanditrocks (Erica)

    This citrus sensation is sure to be a hit! (lemon cake) Ingredients
    • 2 3/4 cups all-purpose flour
    • 2 1/2 teaspoons baking powder
    • 1 teaspoon salt
    • 1 1/2 cups granulated sugar
    • 3/4 cup unsalted butter softened
    • 3 large eggs
    • 1 teaspoon lemon extract
    • 1 1/4 cups whole milk
    • 1 cup powdered sugar sifted
    • 1/3 cup fresh lemon juice
    • 1 cup lemon curd
    • 1 teaspoon golden yellow food color, optional
    (lemon frosting) Ingredients
    • 1 1/2 cups (3 sticks) unsalted butter, softened
    • 4 cups powdered sugar
    • 3 tablespoons cream
    • 2 tablespoons lemon juice
    • 1/2 teaspoon lemon extract
    • 1/4 teaspoon golden yellow food color

    Instructions

    • Preheat the oven to 350 °F. Line 2 muffin trays with cupcake liners.
    • In a large bowl, combine flour, baking powder and salt. In another large bowl or bowl of a stand mixer, cream the sugar and butter until light and fluffly. Add eggs and beat well to combine. Add the lemon extract. On low speed, alternate beating in the flour mixture and the milk until just blended. Add the food coloring and beat on low speed until a consistent color is achieved. Sc r.ape down bowl as needed and re-mix briefly.
    • Scoop the batter into the muffin tins, filling about 2/3 of the way (this recipe will make about 30 cupcakes). Bake 16-18 minutes, or until a toothpick comes out clean. Let cool for 10 minutes.
    • Meanwhile, mix the lemon juice and the powdered sugar. Poke the cupcakes with the tines of a fork, then drizzle the syrup over each cupcake. This adds extra moisture to the cake!
    • For the frosting: in a large bowl, beat together the butter, powdered sugar, heavy cream, lemon juice and lemon extract on low speed until well blended. Beat for 3 minutes on medium speed, sc r.ape down the bowl. Add the golden yellow food color, then beat on high speed until the frosting is light and fluffy, about 2-3 minutes.
    • Frost the cupcakes using the lemon frosting, decorate to taste, and enjoy!
    Chef (Erica) Notes: Recipe originally from Sprinkebakes, my all-time favorite food resource! Recipe is unchanged, except that I simplified it for cupcakes rather than a full cake!

    Fire Rice | Food/lauralie41

    Not only is this rice spicy, it is also aflame! (1,500 NP) Ingredients
    • 2 2⁄3 cups water
    • 1 1⁄3 cups long grain white rice, uncooked
    • 1lb ground pork breakfast sausage
    • 1 (16 ounce) jar picante sauce
    • 1 (8 ounce) container sour cream
    • 8 ounces cheddar cheese, shredded

    Instructions

    • Preheat oven to 350 degrees F.
    • Bring water to boil in a medium saucepan. Stir in the rice, reduce heat, cover, and simmer for approximately 20 minutes.
    • In a large sk1llet over medium heat brown sausage until no longer pink.
    • In a medium mixing bowl add cooked rice, cooked sausage, picante sauce, and sour cream. Mix well, place in casserole dish, and top with cheddar cheese.
    • Bake approximately 20 minutes or until cheese is bubbly. Serve with sides of extra picante sauce and sour cream.

    TRADITIONAL AltadorIAN GYRO | amonsunamun

    delicious gyro with an Altadorian design. -amonsunamun
    • 1 wrap, tortilla or pita per gyro
    • 1/4 to 1/3 cup cooked lamb or beef (vegetarian/vegan substitute okay)
    • 1 tablespoon tzatziki sauce (see note) or plain, unsweetened yogurt (vegan yogurt is fine)
    • Two pieces of thickly-sliced carrot
    • 1/8 tablespoon each powdered cinnamon, coriander seed, rosemary, and oregano
    • Leafy green of your choice, 1 large leaf (or more if you like)
    • 1/4 cup onion very thinly-sliced
    • Olive oil (just a drizzle)
    • Carrot greens or fresh parsley (optional)

    instructions

    • In a nonstick pan on medium-low heat (or a regular pan with a little cooking oil or cooking spray added), add lamb/beef and sliced onions Cook until heated through. Remove from heat, add a drizzle of olive oil and coat well. Add the cinnamon, coriander seed, rosemary and oregano mixture, coat well. Add salt and pepper if you like.
    • On your tortilla/wrap/pita, place your leafy green, carrots, tzatziki or yogurt, and cooked, seasoned meat. Wrap the gyro by folding either end over the middle.
      If using a stick of fresh parsely or carrot greens, wrap around the gyro to match the picture. This is completely edible, healthy and looks nice as well.
    NOTE: Many shops carry tzatziki sauce. If you can't find it, or you'd like to make your own, take 1 cup of unsweetened, plain Greek-style yogurt and mix it with 1 clove of minced garlic and about 1/4 cup of peeled, diced, drained cuke. Mix well, add in a little vinegar or lemon juice to taste (very little will do), then refrigerate for at least two hours to let the flavours really come together.

    HERO GYRO | amonsunamun
    This tasty treat is named after the heroes of Altador! Its just a marketing scheme really. -amonsunamun

    Enjoy!
    • 1 wrap, tortilla or pita per gyro
    • 1/4 to 1/3 cup cooked chicken or vegetarian/vegan substitute
    • 1 tablespoon tzatziki sauce (see note) or plain, unsweetened yogurt (vegan yogurt is fine)
    • 1 tablespoon tomato, diced
    • 1/8 tablespoon each powdered cinnamon, coriander seed, rosemary, and oregano
    • Leafy green of your choice, 1 large leaf (or more if you like)

    instructions

    • Using a pan or the microwave, heat chicken until warm. Coat with the mixture of cinnamon, coriander seed, rosemary, and oregano. Taste it and adjust to your liking.
    • In the middle of your wrap/tortilla/pita, add the leafy green, chicken, tomato, and sauce/yogurt. Wrap and enjoy!

    Altador STYLE BRATWURST | amonsunamun
    No one is really sure what the Altador style of Bratwurst is, but it sure is tasty! -amonsunamun

    Enjoy!
    • 1 bratwurst of your choice, cooked the way you like it (veggie bratwurst also works)
    • 1 whole wheat hot dog bun (or hot dog bun of your choice)
    • 1 tablespoon of your favorite hummus
    • 1/4 large, red sweet pepper, thinly sliced
    • 1 tablespoon onion diced

    • 1 clove garlic, diced

    instructions
